Here is python code that generates similar data 

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Sample data
data = {
    'Organisation': ['PayPal', 'Stripe', 'Square', 'Robinhood', 'Credit Suisse'],
    'Founders': ['Peter Thiel, Max Levchin, Elon Musk', 'Patrick Collison, John Collison', 'Jack Dorsey, Jim McKelvey', 'Baiju Bhatt, Vlad Tenev', 'Alfred P. Kelly, Émile Hottinger'],
    'Market Capitalisation (INR)': [433941, 346939, 254941, 235935, 217439],
    'International Location': ['San Jose, USA', 'San Francisco, USA', 'San Francisco, USA', 'Menlo Park, USA', 'Zurich, Switzerland']
}

# Create DataFrame
df = pd.DataFrame(data)

# Rank the data
df['Rank'] = np.arange(1, len(df) + 1)

# Reorder columns
df = df[['Rank', 'Organisation', 'Founders', 'Market Capitalisation (INR)', 'International Location']]

# Print the DataFrame
print(df)
```

This will generate a similar table with sample data. You can modify the code to include more data and complex logic.
